2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`

4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Django URL Patterns Migration from patterns() to list

## Your Task

Find all Python source files in django/django that implement URL routing: the removed patterns() function (pre-1.10), the current urlpatterns list handling, the include() function, and the URL dispatcher that processes both legacy and current URL definitions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/django--674eda1c.

**Core URL routing files (django/urls/):**
1. `django/urls/__init__.py` - Package init, exports all URL-related symbols
2. `django/urls/conf.py` - Contains `include()`, `path()`, `re_path()`, `_path()` functions
3. `django/urls/resolvers.py` - Contains `URLResolver`, `URLPattern`, `RegexPattern`, `RoutePattern`, `LocalePrefixPattern`, `ResolverMatch`, `get_resolver`, `get_ns_resolver` - the main URL dispatcher
4. `django/urls/base.py` - Contains `resolve()`, `reverse()`, `set_urlconf()`, `get_urlconf()`, etc.
5. `django/urls/converters.py` - URL path converters (IntConverter, StringConverter, etc.)
6. `django/urls/exceptions.py` - `Resolver404`, `NoReverseMatch`
7. `django/urls/utils.py` - `get_callable()`, `get_mod_func()`

**URL configuration files (django/conf/urls/):**
8. `django/conf/urls/__init__.py` - Exports `include`, handler400/403/404/500
9. `django/conf/urls/i18n.py` - `i18n_patterns()`, `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`
10. `django/conf/urls/static.py` - `static()` helper function

**URL checks:**
11. `django/core/checks/urls.py` - URL configuration checks

**Other URL-related files:**
12. `django/contrib/staticfiles/urls.py` - Static files URL patterns

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Django URL Routing: Migration from `patterns()` to list

### Key Files Found

**Core URL routing (`django/urls/`):**
- **`django/urls/conf.py`** — Contains `include()`, `path()`, `re_path()`, and `_path()` — the primary functions for building URL patterns
- **`django/urls/resolvers.py`** — The main URL dispatcher with `URLResolver`, `URLPattern`, `RegexPattern`, `RoutePattern`, `LocalePrefixPattern`, `ResolverMatch`, `get_resolver()`, `get_ns_resolver()`
- **`django/urls/base.py`** — High-level `resolve()`, `reverse()`, `set_urlconf()`, `get_urlconf()`
- **`django/urls/__init__.py`** — Package exports
- **`django/urls/converters.py`** — Path converters (int, str, uuid, slug, path)
- **`django/urls/exceptions.py`** — `Resolver404`, `NoReverseMatch`
- **`django/urls/utils.py`** — `get_callable()`, `get_mod_func()`

**URL configuration (`django/conf/urls/`):**
- **`django/conf/urls/__init__.py`** — Legacy module; now only exports `include` and error handlers (no more `patterns()`)
- **`django/conf/urls/i18n.py`** — `i18n_patterns()`, `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`
- **`django/conf/urls/static.py`** — `static()` helper

**URL checks:**
- **`django/core/checks/urls.py`** — Validates URL config; `get_warning_for_invalid_pattern()` explicitly detects legacy string prefixes and tuples (remnants of the old `patterns()` API)

**Other:**
- **`django/contrib/staticfiles/urls.py`** — `staticfiles_urlpatterns()` helper

### Migration Summary
The `patterns()` function (originally in `django.conf.urls.defaults`, later `django.conf.urls`) was removed in Django 1.10. The current system uses plain Python lists (`urlpatterns = [path(...), re_path(...)]`). The `URLResolver.url_patterns` 
... (truncated)

Overview\\n\\nThe Django codebase in `sg-evals/django--674eda1c` represents a post-1.10 version where the legacy `patterns()` function has been fully removed. The URL routing system is organized across several key files.\\n\\n### The Removed `patterns()` Function (pre-1.10)\\n\\nThe `patterns()` function originally lived in `django/conf/urls/defaults.py` (later moved to `django/conf/urls/__init__.py`). It was deprecated in Django 1.8 and removed in Django 1.10. In this codebase, it no longer exists. The `django/conf/urls/__init__.py` now only exports `include` (re-exported from `django.urls`) and the error handler defaults (`handler400`, `handler403`, `handler404`, `handler500`). The `django/core/checks/urls.py` file contains `get_warning_for_invalid_pattern()` which explicitly warns users when they pass a string prefix (the old `patterns()` first argument) or a tuple (old-style URL tuple) instead of proper `path()`/`re_path()` instances.\\n\\n### Current `urlpatterns` List Handling\\n\\nThe current system uses a plain Python list named `urlpatterns`. The key files are:\\n\\n1. **`django/urls/resolvers.py`** \u2014 The main URL dispatcher. The `URLResolver` class has a `url_patterns` cached property (line 727) that reads `getattr(self.urlconf_module, 'urlpatterns', self.urlconf_module)` \u2014 this is where the `urlpatterns` list is consumed. The `URLResolver.resolve()` method iterates over `url_patterns` to match incoming paths.\\n\\n2. **`django/urls/conf.py`** \u2014 Contains the `include()` function which also reads `getattr(urlconf_module, 'urlpatterns', urlconf_module)` when processing included URL modules. Also defines `_path()`, `path()` (using `RoutePattern`), and `re_path()` (using `RegexPattern`) \u2014 the functions used to build entries in the `urlpatterns` list.\\n\\n### The `include()` Function\\n\\nDefined in **`django/urls/conf.py`** (line 17). It accepts:\\n- A string (module path), list/tuple of patterns, or a 2-tuple `(patterns, app_name)`\\n- An optional `namespace` argument\\n\\nIt returns a 3-tuple `(urlconf_module, app_name, namespace)` which `_path()` then uses to create a `URLResolver` instance.\\n\\n### The URL Dispatcher\\n\\n**`django/urls/resolvers.py`** is the core dispatcher containing:\\n- `URLResolver` \u2014 resolves URL paths by iterating `url_patterns`, handles namespaces, reverse lookups\\n- `URLPattern` \u2014 leaf pattern matching a single view callable\\n- `RegexPattern` \u2014 regex-based URL matching (used by `re_path()`)\\n- `RoutePattern` \u2014 path-converter-based URL matching (used by `path()`)\\n- `LocalePrefixPattern` \u2014 for i18n URL prefixing\\n- `ResolverMatch` \u2014 result object returned by `resolve()`\\n- `get_resolver()` / `get_ns_resolver()` \u2014 cached resolver factory functions\\n\\n### Supporting Files\\n\\n- **`django/urls/__init__.py`** \u2014 Package init that re-exports all public URL API symbols\\n- **`django/urls/base.py`** \u2014 High-level `resolve()`, `reverse()`, `set_urlconf()`, `get_urlconf()` functions\\n- **`django/urls/converters.py`** \u2014 Path converters (`IntConverter`, `StringConverter`, `UUIDConverter`, `SlugConverter`, `PathConverter`) and `register_converter()`\\n- **`django/urls/exceptions.py`** \u2014 `Resolver404` and `NoReverseMatch` exceptions\\n- **`django/urls/utils.py`** \u2014 `get_callable()` and `get_mod_func()` utilities\\n- **`django/conf/urls/__init__.py`** \u2014 Legacy `django.conf.urls` module; exports `include` and error handlers\\n- **`django/conf/urls/i18n.py`** \u2014 `i18n_patterns()` and `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()` for internationalized URL prefixes\\n- **`django/conf/urls/static.py`** \u2014 `static()` helper for serving static files in debug mode\\n- **`django/core/checks/urls.py`** \u2014 System checks for URL configuration validity, including detection of legacy patterns (strings, tuples) that should be `path()`/`re_path()` instances\\n- **`django/contrib/staticfiles/urls.py`** \u2014 `staticfiles_urlpatterns()` helper\"\n    56\t}\n    57\t\n"

formerly contained `patterns()` (removed in Django 1.10), now only exports `include` and error handlers\n- **`django/conf/urls/i18n.py`** \u2014 `i18n_patterns()`, `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`\n- **`django/conf/urls/static.py`** \u2014 `static()` helper\n\n### URL Validation\n- **`django/core/checks/urls.py`** \u2014 System checks including `get_warning_for_invalid_pattern()` which detects legacy string prefixes and tuples (remnants of the old `patterns()` API)\n\n### Contrib URL Files\n- **`django/contrib/staticfiles/urls.py`** \u2014 `staticfiles_urlpatterns()`\n- **`django/contrib/admindocs/urls.py`** and **`views.py`** \u2014 Admin docs URL patterns and `extract_views_from_urlpatterns()`\n- **`django/contrib/auth/urls.py`** \u2014 Auth URL patterns\n- **`django/contrib/flatpages/urls.py`** \u2014 Flatpages URL patterns\n- **`django/contrib/admin/sites.py`** \u2014 Admin site URL generation via `get_urls()`\n- **`django/conf/project_template/project_name/urls.py-tpl`** \u2014 Project template showing the modern `urlpatterns` list pattern\n\n### Key Migration Point\nThe `patterns()` function (originally in `django.conf.urls.defaults`, later `django.conf.urls`) was removed in Django 1.10. The current system uses plain Python lists (`urlpatterns = [path(...), re_path(...)]`). The `URLResolver.url_patterns` property in `resolvers.py` reads the `urlpatterns` attribute from URL modules, and `include()` in `conf.py` handles both string module paths and list/tuple patterns."
